In [1]:
import pandas as pd
import json
In [2]:
df=pd.read_csv("sfpd_dispatch_data_subset.csv")
In [3]:
dispatches= pd.DataFrame(df['received_timestamp'])
In [4]:
dispatches['address']= df['address']
In [5]:
dispatches['unit_type']=df['unit_type'] #hold values in new dataframe
In [6]:
dispatches.set_index('received_timestamp', inplace=True)
In [7]:
d_dict=dispatches.to_dict('index')
In [8]:
for key in d_dict.keys(): #go through all keys to convert to string
  if type(key) is not str:
    try:
      d_dict[str(key)] = d_dict[key]
    except:
      try:
        d_dict[repr(key)] = d_dict[key]
      except:
        pass
    del d_dict[key]
In [11]:
json.dumps(d_dict)
